# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Pants
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Legs
- Color: Blue
- Stat Buffs
    - Defense DC ✦ = L
    - Movement Speed ✦ = Lx2
    - HP = Lx1.5
    - Armor = L÷2
- Actives:
    - [Leaden Target](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Leaden+Target)
    - [Fight Me](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Fight+Me)
    - You have access to Tiers I-III of each of your Actives.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Pirate)

- Color: Blue
